Leahi Bla Pahinui Taro Patch (DGDGBD) Gabby (the “Brown Album) (Panini Records 1002) – [with Bla playing nylon string guitar backing up Gabby Pahinui; Gabby on 12 string guitar] The introduction is played on nylon string guitar by Bla Pahinui in the G Major Tuning (# G1: D-G-D-G-B-D), played in the key of C, and tuned down one half step to sound in the key of B. Gabby Pahinui plays the 12 string guitar in the C Wahine Tuning (#C11: C-G-E-G-B-E), tuned down one half step to sound in the key of B.
Lei No Ka`iulani Bla Pahinui Taro Patch (DGDGBD) Gabby (the “Brown Album) (Panini Records 1002) – [with Bla playing nylon string guitar backing up Gabby Pahinui; Gabby on 12 string guitar] The introduction is played on nylon string guitar by Bla Pahinui in the G Major Tuning (# G1: D-G-D-G-B-D), capoed up three frets to sound in the key of Bb. Gabby Pahinui plays the 12 string guitar in the C Mauna Loa Tuning (# C22: C-G-E-G-A-E), tuned down two half steps to sound in the key of Bb.
Lihue Bla Pahinui Taro Patch (DGDGBD) Gabby (the “Brown Album) (Panini Records 1002) – [with Bla playing nylon string guitar backing up Gabby Pahinui; Gabby on 12 string guitar] The introduction and the ending are played on nylon string guitar by Bla Pahinui in the G Major Tuning (# G1: D-G-D-G-B-D), and the intro and the ending use the chords D minor to G, resolving to C, capoed up one fret to sound in the key of C#. Gabby Pahinui plays the 12 string guitar in the C Wahine Tining (#C11: C-G-E-G-B-E), capoed up one half step to sound in the key of C#.

Alma Mater Medley: Pahoa and Pahala High Schools Led Kaapana Standard (EADGBE) Simply Slack Key (Paradise Records 970) – On these songs, the Slack Key guitar part is listed as the main guitar part. The second guitar part is played on electric guitar in Standard Tuning. Led always plays in Standard Tuning on the electric guitar The main Slack Key guitar part is in C Wahine Tuning (#C7: C–G–D–G–B–E).

So Ti Manu Kahaialii (with the Kahaialii Family) Standard (EADGBE) Kahaialii Maui Style (Naupaka Records 0001) Played in the key of D. This song also features Manu’s unique right hand hammer-on and pull-off techniques on the D and A7th chords, called ha ku`iku`i. His son, Willie K plays this song also in the Standard Tuning, in the key of C, with the technique used of the C and G7th chords. (also see Section VII, the glossery, under ha ku`iku`i)

Hawaiian Love Bla Pahinui Standard (EADGBE) The Gabby Pahinui Hawaiian Band – Volume 1 [backing up Gabby Pahinui] (Panini Records 1007; also issued on Warner Brothers Records 3023 – out-of-print) Bla plays the nylon string guitar in the Standard Tuning, key of C, capoed up two frets to sound in the key of D.
Pu’uwa’a-awa’a Bla Pahinui Standard (EADGBE) The Gabby Pahinui Hawaiian Band – Volume 2 (Panini Records 1008) – Gabby on 12 string guitar Bla plays the introduction on the nylonstring guitar in the Standard Tuning, fingering in the keys of G and Eb, and is capoed up eight frets, therefore sounding in the keys of E and C. Gabby Pahinui plays the 12 string guitar in the C Mauna Loa Tuning (#C22: C-G-E-G-A-E).
Paauau Waltz Gabby Pahinui Standard (EADGBE) Hawaiian Slack Key – Volume 1 – With Gabby Pahinui Here Gabby Pahinui is playing this song with the ensamble in the Standard Tuning, in the keys of F and Ab, and uses the technique called ha ku`iku`i at the end of the song for variations on the chords of F# and E, before going back to the final Ab chord at the end of the song. (also see Section VII, the Glossery, under ha ku`iku`i)
Makawao Jeff Peterson Standard (EADGBE) Slack Key Guitar: The Artistry of Jeff Peterson (Palm Records PALM4025) Played in the key of E – tuned down a half step to sound in the key of Eb.
Slack Key Instrumental #2 Fred Punahoa Standard (EADGBE) Waimea Music Festival [Anthology Recording] (Panini Records 1006) (actual title is Mauna Loa Slack Key) – Played in the key of A.
Matsonia Vicki I`i Rodrigues (with her daughters Lani, Lahela & Nina Kealiiwahamana on vocals) Standard (EADGBE) Hawaii Aloha: Echoes of Old Hawaii (Waikiki Records 307) Played in the key of C.
Pua Carnation Vicki I`i Rodrigues (with her daughters Lani, Lahela & Nina Kealiiwahamana on vocals) Standard (EADGBE) Hawaii Aloha: Echoes of Old Hawaii (Waikiki Records 307) Played in the key of C. This track also appears on the anthology album Quiet Lagoon (Waikiki Records 333).
Kane`ohe Vicki I`i Rodrigues (with her daughters Lani, Lahela & Nina Kealiiwahamana on vocals) Standard (EADGBE) Party Hulas Featuring the Voice of Genoa Keawe (London International 99397)
`E Ku`u Tutu Vicki I`i Rodrigues (with her daughters Lani, Lahela & Nina Kealiiwahamana on vocals) Standard (EADGBE) Mele–Hula Volume Two (Noelani Records 103) Played in the key of A.
Lei Nani Vicki I`i Rodrigues (with her daughters Lani, Lahela & Nina Kealiiwahamana on vocals) Standard (EADGBE) Genoa Keawe Sings Luau Hulas [backing up Genoa Keawe] (Hula Records 514 – out-of-print) Played in the key of C.
Makee Ailana Vicki I`i Rodrigues (with her daughters Lani, Lahela & Nina Kealiiwahamana on vocals) Standard (EADGBE) Genoa Keawe Sings Luau Hulas [backing up Genoa Keawe] (Hula Records 514 – out-of-print) Played in the key of C.
Meleana E Vicki I`i Rodrigues (with her daughters Lani, Lahela & Nina Kealiiwahamana on vocals) Standard (EADGBE) Genoa Keawe Sings Luau Hulas [backing up Genoa Keawe] (Hula Records 514 – out-of-print) Played in the key of C.
